EXACT SYMBOLIC EIGENVALUES
==========================

Spectrum k=0:
--------------------
Lambda_1:
4*a^2*b^2/c^2

Lambda_2:
4*a^2*c^2/b^2

Lambda_3:
4*b^2*c^2/a^2

Spectrum k=1:
--------------------
Lambda_1:
(2*a^4*b^4 + a^4*b^2*c^2 + a^2*b^4*c^2 + 2*a^4*c^4 + a^2*b^2*c^4 + 2*b^4*c^4 - 2*sqrt(a^4*b^4 + (a^4 - a^2*b^2 + b^4)*c^4 - (a^4*b^2 + a^2*b^4)*c^2)*a^2*b^2 - 2*sqrt(a^4*b^4 + (a^4 - a^2*b^2 + b^4)*c^4 - (a^4*b^2 + a^2*b^4)*c^2)*a^2*c^2 - 2*sqrt(a^4*b^4 + (a^4 - a^2*b^2 + b^4)*c^4 - (a^4*b^2 + a^2*b^4)*c^2)*b^2*c^2)/(a^2*b^2*c^2)

Lambda_2:
(2*a^4*b^4 + a^4*b^2*c^2 + a^2*b^4*c^2 + 2*a^4*c^4 + a^2*b^2*c^4 + 2*b^4*c^4 - 2*sqrt(a^4*b^4 + (a^4 - a^2*b^2 + b^4)*c^4 - (a^4*b^2 + a^2*b^4)*c^2)*a^2*b^2 - 2*sqrt(a^4*b^4 + (a^4 - a^2*b^2 + b^4)*c^4 - (a^4*b^2 + a^2*b^4)*c^2)*a^2*c^2 - 2*sqrt(a^4*b^4 + (a^4 - a^2*b^2 + b^4)*c^4 - (a^4*b^2 + a^2*b^4)*c^2)*b^2*c^2)/(a^2*b^2*c^2)

Lambda_3:
(2*a^4*b^4 + a^4*b^2*c^2 + a^2*b^4*c^2 + 2*a^4*c^4 + a^2*b^2*c^4 + 2*b^4*c^4 + 2*sqrt(a^4*b^4 + (a^4 - a^2*b^2 + b^4)*c^4 - (a^4*b^2 + a^2*b^4)*c^2)*a^2*b^2 + 2*sqrt(a^4*b^4 + (a^4 - a^2*b^2 + b^4)*c^4 - (a^4*b^2 + a^2*b^4)*c^2)*a^2*c^2 + 2*sqrt(a^4*b^4 + (a^4 - a^2*b^2 + b^4)*c^4 - (a^4*b^2 + a^2*b^4)*c^2)*b^2*c^2)/(a^2*b^2*c^2)

Lambda_4:
(2*a^4*b^4 + a^4*b^2*c^2 + a^2*b^4*c^2 + 2*a^4*c^4 + a^2*b^2*c^4 + 2*b^4*c^4 + 2*sqrt(a^4*b^4 + (a^4 - a^2*b^2 + b^4)*c^4 - (a^4*b^2 + a^2*b^4)*c^2)*a^2*b^2 + 2*sqrt(a^4*b^4 + (a^4 - a^2*b^2 + b^4)*c^4 - (a^4*b^2 + a^2*b^4)*c^2)*a^2*c^2 + 2*sqrt(a^4*b^4 + (a^4 - a^2*b^2 + b^4)*c^4 - (a^4*b^2 + a^2*b^4)*c^2)*b^2*c^2)/(a^2*b^2*c^2)

Lambda_5:
a^2 + b^2 + c^2

Lambda_6:
a^2 + b^2 + c^2
